.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:122:      const topTotalLengthM = beamLengthM * beamTopNos * beamNos;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:123:      beamTopWeight = topTotalLengthM * getWeightPerMeter(beamTopDia);
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:125:      const bottomTotalLengthM = beamLengthM * beamBottomNos * beamNos;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:126:      beamBottomWeight = bottomTotalLengthM * getWeightPerMeter(beamBottomDia);
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:130:      const stirrupNosTotal = Math.floor(beamLengthM / (stirrupSpacing / 1000)) + 1;

.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:132:      stirrupWeight = stirrupTotalLengthM * getWeightPerMeter(stirrupDia);
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:135:    const totalSteelKg = mainBarWeightWithWastage + distBarWeightWithWastage + beamTopWeight + beamBottomWeight + stirrupWeight;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:137:    // Concrete Volume
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:138:    const slabVolumeCft = length * width * (thickness / 304.8) * slabNos;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:139:    let beamVolumeCft = 0;

.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:147:    // Concrete Materials

.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:152:    const aggregate12Cft = aggregateTotalCft * 0.4;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:155:    const bindingWire = totalSteelKg * 0.008;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:156:    const coverBlocks = totalVolumeCum * 20;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:157:    const waterLtr = cementBags * 50 * 0.45;
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:159:    // Material Costs using dynamic rates

.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:162:    const agg20Cost = aggregate20Cft * (rates?.aggregate20 || 50);
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:163:    const agg12Cost = aggregate12Cft * (rates?.aggregate12 || 48);

.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:165:    const bindingWireCost = bindingWire * (rates?.bindingWire || 80);
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:166:    const coverBlockCost = coverBlocks * (rates?.coverBlock || 5);
.\pages\rcc-slab-calculator.tsx:167:    const waterCost = waterLtr * (rates?.water || 0.5);
